22// This header file defines implementation details of how the trace macros in
23// trace_event_common.h collect and store trace events. Anything not
24// implementation-specific should go in trace_macros_common.h instead of here.
25
26
27// The pointer returned from GetCategoryGroupEnabled() points to a
28// value with zero or more of the following bits. Used in this class only.
29// The TRACE_EVENT macros should only use the value as a bool.
30// These values must be in sync with macro values in trace_log.h in
31// chromium.
32enum CategoryGroupEnabledFlags {
33 // Category group enabled for the recording mode.
34 kEnabledForRecording_CategoryGroupEnabledFlags = 1 << 0,
35 // Category group enabled by SetEventCallbackEnabled().
36 kEnabledForEventCallback_CategoryGroupEnabledFlags = 1 << 2,
37 // Category group enabled to export events to ETW.
38 kEnabledForETWExport_CategoryGroupEnabledFlags = 1 << 3,
39};
40

64////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
65// Implementation specific tracing API definitions.
66
67// Get a pointer to the enabled state of the given trace category. Only
68// long-lived literal strings should be given as the category group. The
69// returned pointer can be held permanently in a local static for example. If
70// the unsigned char is non-zero, tracing is enabled. If tracing is enabled,
71// TRACE_EVENT_API_ADD_TRACE_EVENT can be called. It's OK if tracing is disabled
72// between the load of the tracing state and the call to
73// TRACE_EVENT_API_ADD_TRACE_EVENT, because this flag only provides an early out
74// for best performance when tracing is disabled.
75// const uint8_t*
76// TRACE_EVENT_API_GET_CATEGORY_GROUP_ENABLED(const char* category_group)
77#define TRACE_EVENT_API_GET_CATEGORY_GROUP_ENABLEDv8::internal::tracing::TraceEventHelper::GetTracingController
() ->GetCategoryGroupEnabled \
78 v8::internal::tracing::TraceEventHelper::GetTracingController() \
79 ->GetCategoryGroupEnabled
80

306// TraceID encapsulates an ID that can either be an integer or pointer.
307class TraceID {
308 public:
309 class WithScope {
310 public:
311 WithScope(const char* scope, uint64_t raw_id)
312 : scope_(scope), raw_id_(raw_id) {}
313 uint64_t raw_id() const { return raw_id_; }
314 const char* scope() const { return scope_; }
315
316 private:
317 const char* scope_ = nullptr;
318 uint64_t raw_id_;
319 };
320
321 TraceID(const void* raw_id, unsigned int* flags)
322 : raw_id_(static_cast<uint64_t>(reinterpret_cast<uintptr_t>(raw_id))) {}
323 TraceID(uint64_t raw_id, unsigned int* flags) : raw_id_(raw_id) {
324 (void)flags;
325 }
326 TraceID(unsigned int raw_id, unsigned int* flags) : raw_id_(raw_id) {
327 (void)flags;
328 }
329 TraceID(uint16_t raw_id, unsigned int* flags) : raw_id_(raw_id) {
330 (void)flags;
331 }
332 TraceID(unsigned char raw_id, unsigned int* flags) : raw_id_(raw_id) {
333 (void)flags;
334 }
335 TraceID(int64_t raw_id, unsigned int* flags)
336 : raw_id_(static_cast<uint64_t>(raw_id)) {
337 (void)flags;
338 }
339 TraceID(int raw_id, unsigned int* flags)
340 : raw_id_(static_cast<uint64_t>(raw_id)) {
341 (void)flags;
342 }
343 TraceID(int16_t raw_id, unsigned int* flags)
344 : raw_id_(static_cast<uint64_t>(raw_id)) {
345 (void)flags;
346 }
347 TraceID(signed char raw_id, unsigned int* flags)
348 : raw_id_(static_cast<uint64_t>(raw_id)) {
349 (void)flags;
350 }
351 TraceID(WithScope scoped_id, unsigned int* flags)
352 : scope_(scoped_id.scope()), raw_id_(scoped_id.raw_id()) {}
353
354 uint64_t raw_id() const { return raw_id_; }
355 const char* scope() const { return scope_; }
356
357 private:
358 const char* scope_ = nullptr;
359 uint64_t raw_id_;
360};

372static V8_INLINEinline __attribute__((always_inline)) uint64_t AddTraceEventImpl(
373 char phase, const uint8_t* category_group_enabled, const char* name,
374 const char* scope, uint64_t id, uint64_t bind_id, int32_t num_args,
375 const char** arg_names, const uint8_t* arg_types,
376 const uint64_t* arg_values, unsigned int flags) {
377 std::unique_ptr<ConvertableToTraceFormat> arg_convertables[2];
378 if (num_args > 0 && arg_types[0] == TRACE_VALUE_TYPE_CONVERTABLE(static_cast<unsigned char>(8))) {
379 arg_convertables[0].reset(reinterpret_cast<ConvertableToTraceFormat*>(
380 static_cast<intptr_t>(arg_values[0])));
381 }
382 if (num_args > 1 && arg_types[1] == TRACE_VALUE_TYPE_CONVERTABLE(static_cast<unsigned char>(8))) {
383 arg_convertables[1].reset(reinterpret_cast<ConvertableToTraceFormat*>(
384 static_cast<intptr_t>(arg_values[1])));
385 }
386 DCHECK_LE(num_args, 2)((void) 0);
387 v8::TracingController* controller =
388 v8::internal::tracing::TraceEventHelper::GetTracingController();
389 return controller->AddTraceEvent(phase, category_group_enabled, name, scope,
390 id, bind_id, num_args, arg_names, arg_types,
391 arg_values, arg_convertables, flags);
392}

394static V8_INLINEinline __attribute__((always_inline)) uint64_t AddTraceEventWithTimestampImpl(
395 char phase, const uint8_t* category_group_enabled, const char* name,
396 const char* scope, uint64_t id, uint64_t bind_id, int32_t num_args,
397 const char** arg_names, const uint8_t* arg_types,
398 const uint64_t* arg_values, unsigned int flags, int64_t timestamp) {
399 std::unique_ptr<ConvertableToTraceFormat> arg_convertables[2];
400 if (num_args > 0 && arg_types[0] == TRACE_VALUE_TYPE_CONVERTABLE(static_cast<unsigned char>(8))) {
401 arg_convertables[0].reset(reinterpret_cast<ConvertableToTraceFormat*>(
402 static_cast<intptr_t>(arg_values[0])));
403 }
404 if (num_args > 1 && arg_types[1] == TRACE_VALUE_TYPE_CONVERTABLE(static_cast<unsigned char>(8))) {
405 arg_convertables[1].reset(reinterpret_cast<ConvertableToTraceFormat*>(
406 static_cast<intptr_t>(arg_values[1])));
407 }
408 DCHECK_LE(num_args, 2)((void) 0);
409 v8::TracingController* controller =
410 v8::internal::tracing::TraceEventHelper::GetTracingController();
411 return controller->AddTraceEventWithTimestamp(
412 phase, category_group_enabled, name, scope, id, bind_id, num_args,
413 arg_names, arg_types, arg_values, arg_convertables, flags, timestamp);
414}

416// Define SetTraceValue for each allowed type. It stores the type and
417// value in the return arguments. This allows this API to avoid declaring any
418// structures so that it is portable to third_party libraries.
419// This is the base implementation for integer types (including bool) and enums.
420template <typename T>
421static V8_INLINEinline __attribute__((always_inline)) typename std::enable_if<
422 std::is_integral<T>::value || std::is_enum<T>::value, void>::type
423SetTraceValue(T arg, unsigned char* type, uint64_t* value) {
424 *type = std::is_same<T, bool>::value
425 ? TRACE_VALUE_TYPE_BOOL(static_cast<unsigned char>(1))
426 : std::is_signed<T>::value ? TRACE_VALUE_TYPE_INT(static_cast<unsigned char>(3))
427 : TRACE_VALUE_TYPE_UINT(static_cast<unsigned char>(2));
428 *value = static_cast<uint64_t>(arg);
429}
430
431#define INTERNAL_DECLARE_SET_TRACE_VALUE(actual_type, value_type_id) \
432 static V8_INLINEinline __attribute__((always_inline)) void SetTraceValue(actual_type arg, unsigned char* type, \
433 uint64_t* value) { \
434 *type = value_type_id; \
435 *value = 0; \
436 STATIC_ASSERT(sizeof(arg) <= sizeof(*value))static_assert(sizeof(arg) <= sizeof(*value), "sizeof(arg) <= sizeof(*value)"
); \
437 memcpy(value, &arg, sizeof(arg)); \
438 }
439INTERNAL_DECLARE_SET_TRACE_VALUE(double, TRACE_VALUE_TYPE_DOUBLE(static_cast<unsigned char>(4)))
440INTERNAL_DECLARE_SET_TRACE_VALUE(const void*, TRACE_VALUE_TYPE_POINTER(static_cast<unsigned char>(5)))
441INTERNAL_DECLARE_SET_TRACE_VALUE(const char*, TRACE_VALUE_TYPE_STRING(static_cast<unsigned char>(6)))
442INTERNAL_DECLARE_SET_TRACE_VALUE(const TraceStringWithCopy&,
443 TRACE_VALUE_TYPE_COPY_STRING(static_cast<unsigned char>(7)))
444#undef INTERNAL_DECLARE_SET_TRACE_VALUE
445
446static V8_INLINEinline __attribute__((always_inline)) void SetTraceValue(ConvertableToTraceFormat* convertable_value,
447 unsigned char* type, uint64_t* value) {
448 *type = TRACE_VALUE_TYPE_CONVERTABLE(static_cast<unsigned char>(8));
449 *value = static_cast<uint64_t>(reinterpret_cast<intptr_t>(convertable_value));
450}
451
452template <typename T>
453static V8_INLINEinline __attribute__((always_inline)) typename std::enable_if<
454 std::is_convertible<T*, ConvertableToTraceFormat*>::value>::type
455SetTraceValue(std::unique_ptr<T> ptr, unsigned char* type, uint64_t* value) {
456 SetTraceValue(ptr.release(), type, value);
457}
458
459// These AddTraceEvent template
460// function is defined here instead of in the macro, because the arg_values
461// could be temporary objects, such as std::string. In order to store
462// pointers to the internal c_str and pass through to the tracing API,
463// the arg_values must live throughout these procedures.
464
465static V8_INLINEinline __attribute__((always_inline)) uint64_t AddTraceEvent(char phase,
466 const uint8_t* category_group_enabled,
467 const char* name, const char* scope,
468 uint64_t id, uint64_t bind_id,
469 unsigned int flags) {
470 return TRACE_EVENT_API_ADD_TRACE_EVENTv8::internal::tracing::AddTraceEventImpl(phase, category_group_enabled, name,
471 scope, id, bind_id, kZeroNumArgs,
472 nullptr, nullptr, nullptr, flags);
473}
474
475template <class ARG1_TYPE>
476static V8_INLINEinline __attribute__((always_inline)) uint64_t AddTraceEvent(
477 char phase, const uint8_t* category_group_enabled, const char* name,
478 const char* scope, uint64_t id, uint64_t bind_id, unsigned int flags,
479 const char* arg1_name, ARG1_TYPE&& arg1_val) {
480 const int num_args = 1;
481 uint8_t arg_type;
482 uint64_t arg_value;
483 SetTraceValue(std::forward<ARG1_TYPE>(arg1_val), &arg_type, &arg_value);
484 return TRACE_EVENT_API_ADD_TRACE_EVENTv8::internal::tracing::AddTraceEventImpl(
485 phase, category_group_enabled, name, scope, id, bind_id, num_args,
486 &arg1_name, &arg_type, &arg_value, flags);
487}

489template <class ARG1_TYPE, class ARG2_TYPE>
490static V8_INLINEinline __attribute__((always_inline)) uint64_t AddTraceEvent(
491 char phase, const uint8_t* category_group_enabled, const char* name,
492 const char* scope, uint64_t id, uint64_t bind_id, unsigned int flags,
493 const char* arg1_name, ARG1_TYPE&& arg1_val, const char* arg2_name,
494 ARG2_TYPE&& arg2_val) {
495 const int num_args = 2;
496 const char* arg_names[2] = {arg1_name, arg2_name};
497 unsigned char arg_types[2];
498 uint64_t arg_values[2];
499 SetTraceValue(std::forward<ARG1_TYPE>(arg1_val), &arg_types[0],
500 &arg_values[0]);
501 SetTraceValue(std::forward<ARG2_TYPE>(arg2_val), &arg_types[1],
502 &arg_values[1]);
503 return TRACE_EVENT_API_ADD_TRACE_EVENTv8::internal::tracing::AddTraceEventImpl(
504 phase, category_group_enabled, name, scope, id, bind_id, num_args,
505 arg_names, arg_types, arg_values, flags);
506}

550// Used by TRACE_EVENTx macros. Do not use directly.
551class ScopedTracer {
552 public:
553 // Note: members of data_ intentionally left uninitialized. See Initialize.
554 ScopedTracer() : p_data_(nullptr) {}
7
←
3 uninitialized fields at the end of the constructor call
555
556 ~ScopedTracer() {
557 if (p_data_ && base::Relaxed_Load(reinterpret_cast<const base::Atomic8*>(
558 data_.category_group_enabled))) {
559 TRACE_EVENT_API_UPDATE_TRACE_EVENT_DURATIONv8::internal::tracing::TraceEventHelper::GetTracingController
() ->UpdateTraceEventDuration(
560 data_.category_group_enabled, data_.name, data_.event_handle);
561 }
562 }
563
564 void Initialize(const uint8_t* category_group_enabled, const char* name,
565 uint64_t event_handle) {
566 data_.category_group_enabled = category_group_enabled;
567 data_.name = name;
568 data_.event_handle = event_handle;
569 p_data_ = &data_;
570 }
571
572 private:
573 // This Data struct workaround is to avoid initializing all the members
574 // in Data during construction of this object, since this object is always
575 // constructed, even when tracing is disabled. If the members of Data were
576 // members of this class instead, compiler warnings occur about potential
577 // uninitialized accesses.
578 struct Data {
579 const uint8_t* category_group_enabled;
uninitialized pointer 'this->data_.category_group_enabled'
580 const char* name;
uninitialized pointer 'this->data_.name'
581 uint64_t event_handle;
uninitialized field 'this->data_.event_handle'
582 };
583 Data* p_data_;
584 Data data_;
585};

), 0))) {

604 const char* name;
605 v8::internal::Isolate* isolate;
606 };
607 bool has_parent_scope_;
608 Data* p_data_;
609 Data data_;
610};

26MaybeHandle<Object> Runtime::GetObjectProperty(Isolate* isolate,
27 Handle<Object> object,
28 Handle<Object> key,
29 bool* is_found_out) {
30 if (object->IsNullOrUndefined(isolate)) {
31 ErrorUtils::ThrowLoadFromNullOrUndefined(isolate, object, key);
32 return MaybeHandle<Object>();
33 }
34
35 bool success = false;
36 LookupIterator::Key lookup_key(isolate, key, &success);
37 if (!success) return MaybeHandle<Object>();
38 LookupIterator it(isolate, object, lookup_key);
39
40 MaybeHandle<Object> result = Object::GetProperty(&it);
41 if (is_found_out) *is_found_out = it.IsFound();
42
43 if (!it.IsFound() && key->IsSymbol() &&
44 Symbol::cast(*key).is_private_name()) {
45 Handle<Symbol> sym = Handle<Symbol>::cast(key);
46 Handle<Object> name(sym->description(), isolate);
47 DCHECK(name->IsString())((void) 0);
48 Handle<String> name_string = Handle<String>::cast(name);
49 if (sym->IsPrivateBrand()) {
50 Handle<String> class_name = (name_string->length() == 0)
51 ? isolate->factory()->anonymous_string()
52 : name_string;
53 THROW_NEW_ERROR(isolate,do { auto* __isolate__ = (isolate); return __isolate__->template
Throw<Object>(__isolate__->factory()->NewTypeError
(MessageTemplate::kInvalidPrivateBrand, class_name, object));
} while (false)
54 NewTypeError(MessageTemplate::kInvalidPrivateBrand,do { auto* __isolate__ = (isolate); return __isolate__->template
Throw<Object>(__isolate__->factory()->NewTypeError
(MessageTemplate::kInvalidPrivateBrand, class_name, object));
} while (false)
55 class_name, object),do { auto* __isolate__ = (isolate); return __isolate__->template
Throw<Object>(__isolate__->factory()->NewTypeError
(MessageTemplate::kInvalidPrivateBrand, class_name, object));
} while (false)
56 Object)do { auto* __isolate__ = (isolate); return __isolate__->template
Throw<Object>(__isolate__->factory()->NewTypeError
(MessageTemplate::kInvalidPrivateBrand, class_name, object));
} while (false);
57 }
58 THROW_NEW_ERROR(isolate,do { auto* __isolate__ = (isolate); return __isolate__->template
Throw<Object>(__isolate__->factory()->NewTypeError
(MessageTemplate::kInvalidPrivateMemberRead, name_string, object
)); } while (false)
59 NewTypeError(MessageTemplate::kInvalidPrivateMemberRead,do { auto* __isolate__ = (isolate); return __isolate__->template
Throw<Object>(__isolate__->factory()->NewTypeError
(MessageTemplate::kInvalidPrivateMemberRead, name_string, object
)); } while (false)
60 name_string, object),do { auto* __isolate__ = (isolate); return __isolate__->template
Throw<Object>(__isolate__->factory()->NewTypeError
(MessageTemplate::kInvalidPrivateMemberRead, name_string, object
)); } while (false)
61 Object)do { auto* __isolate__ = (isolate); return __isolate__->template
Throw<Object>(__isolate__->factory()->NewTypeError
(MessageTemplate::kInvalidPrivateMemberRead, name_string, object
)); } while (false);
62 }
63 return result;
64}

66MaybeHandle<Object> Runtime::HasProperty(Isolate* isolate,
67 Handle<Object> object,
68 Handle<Object> key) {
69 // Check that {object} is actually a receiver.
70 if (!object->IsJSReceiver()) {
71 THROW_NEW_ERROR(do { auto* __isolate__ = (isolate); return __isolate__->template
Throw<Object>(__isolate__->factory()->NewTypeError
(MessageTemplate::kInvalidInOperatorUse, key, object)); } while
(false)
72 isolate,do { auto* __isolate__ = (isolate); return __isolate__->template
Throw<Object>(__isolate__->factory()->NewTypeError
(MessageTemplate::kInvalidInOperatorUse, key, object)); } while
(false)
73 NewTypeError(MessageTemplate::kInvalidInOperatorUse, key, object),do { auto* __isolate__ = (isolate); return __isolate__->template
Throw<Object>(__isolate__->factory()->NewTypeError
(MessageTemplate::kInvalidInOperatorUse, key, object)); } while
(false)
74 Object)do { auto* __isolate__ = (isolate); return __isolate__->template
Throw<Object>(__isolate__->factory()->NewTypeError
(MessageTemplate::kInvalidInOperatorUse, key, object)); } while
(false);
75 }
76 Handle<JSReceiver> receiver = Handle<JSReceiver>::cast(object);
77
78 // Convert the {key} to a name.
79 Handle<Name> name;
80 ASSIGN_RETURN_ON_EXCEPTION(isolate, name, Object::ToName(isolate, key),do { if (!(Object::ToName(isolate, key)).ToHandle(&name))
{ ((void) 0); return MaybeHandle<Object>(); } } while (
false)
81 Object)do { if (!(Object::ToName(isolate, key)).ToHandle(&name))
{ ((void) 0); return MaybeHandle<Object>(); } } while (
false);
82
83 // Lookup the {name} on {receiver}.
84 Maybe<bool> maybe = JSReceiver::HasProperty(receiver, name);
85 if (maybe.IsNothing()) return MaybeHandle<Object>();
86 return maybe.FromJust() ? ReadOnlyRoots(isolate).true_value_handle()
87 : ReadOnlyRoots(isolate).false_value_handle();
88}
89
90namespace {
91
92bool DeleteObjectPropertyFast(Isolate* isolate, Handle<JSReceiver> receiver,
93 Handle<Object> raw_key) {
94 // This implements a special case for fast property deletion: when the
95 // last property in an object is deleted, then instead of normalizing
96 // the properties, we can undo the last map transition, with a few
97 // prerequisites:
98 // (1) The receiver must be a regular object and the key a unique name.
99 Handle<Map> receiver_map(receiver->map(), isolate);
100 if (receiver_map->IsSpecialReceiverMap()) return false;
101 if (!raw_key->IsUniqueName()) return false;
102 Handle<Name> key = Handle<Name>::cast(raw_key);
103 // (2) The property to be deleted must be the last property.
104 int nof = receiver_map->NumberOfOwnDescriptors();
105 if (nof == 0) return false;
106 InternalIndex descriptor(nof - 1);
107 Handle<DescriptorArray> descriptors(receiver_map->instance_descriptors(),
108 isolate);
109 if (descriptors->GetKey(descriptor) != *key) return false;
110 // (3) The property to be deleted must be deletable.
111 PropertyDetails details = descriptors->GetDetails(descriptor);
112 if (!details.IsConfigurable()) return false;
113 // (4) The map must have a back pointer.
114 Handle<Object> backpointer(receiver_map->GetBackPointer(), isolate);
115 if (!backpointer->IsMap()) return false;
116 Handle<Map> parent_map = Handle<Map>::cast(backpointer);
117 // (5) The last transition must have been caused by adding a property
118 // (and not any kind of special transition).
119 if (parent_map->NumberOfOwnDescriptors() != nof - 1) return false;
120
121 // Preconditions successful. No more bailouts after this point.
122
123 // If the {descriptor} was "const" so far, we need to update the
124 // {receiver_map} here, otherwise we could get the constants wrong, i.e.
125 //
126 // o.x = 1;
127 // delete o.x;
128 // o.x = 2;
129 //
130 // could trick V8 into thinking that `o.x` is still 1 even after the second
131 // assignment.
132 if (details.constness() == PropertyConstness::kConst &&
133 details.location() == kField) {
134 Handle<FieldType> field_type(descriptors->GetFieldType(descriptor),
135 isolate);
136 Map::GeneralizeField(isolate, receiver_map, descriptor,
137 PropertyConstness::kMutable, details.representation(),
138 field_type);
139 DCHECK_EQ(PropertyConstness::kMutable,((void) 0)
140 descriptors->GetDetails(descriptor).constness())((void) 0);
141 }
142
143 // Zap the property to avoid keeping objects alive. Zapping is not necessary
144 // for properties stored in the descriptor array.
145 if (details.location() == kField) {
146 DisallowHeapAllocation no_allocation;
147
148 // Invalidate slots manually later in case we delete an in-object tagged
149 // property. In this case we might later store an untagged value in the
150 // recorded slot.
151 isolate->heap()->NotifyObjectLayoutChange(*receiver, no_allocation,
152 InvalidateRecordedSlots::kNo);
153 FieldIndex index =
154 FieldIndex::ForPropertyIndex(*receiver_map, details.field_index());
155 // Special case deleting the last out-of object property.
156 if (!index.is_inobject() && index.outobject_array_index() == 0) {
157 DCHECK(!parent_map->HasOutOfObjectProperties())((void) 0);
158 // Clear out the properties backing store.
159 receiver->SetProperties(ReadOnlyRoots(isolate).empty_fixed_array());
160 } else {
161 Object filler = ReadOnlyRoots(isolate).one_pointer_filler_map();
162 JSObject::cast(*receiver).RawFastPropertyAtPut(index, filler);
163 // We must clear any recorded slot for the deleted property, because
164 // subsequent object modifications might put a raw double there.
165 // Slot clearing is the reason why this entire function cannot currently
166 // be implemented in the DeleteProperty stub.
167 if (index.is_inobject() && !receiver_map->IsUnboxedDoubleField(index)) {
168 // We need to clear the recorded slot in this case because in-object
169 // slack tracking might not be finished. This ensures that we don't
170 // have recorded slots in free space.
171 isolate->heap()->ClearRecordedSlot(*receiver,
172 receiver->RawField(index.offset()));
173 MemoryChunk* chunk = MemoryChunk::FromHeapObject(*receiver);
174 chunk->InvalidateRecordedSlots(*receiver);
175 }
176 }
177 }
178 // If the {receiver_map} was marked stable before, then there could be
179 // optimized code that depends on the assumption that no object that
180 // reached this {receiver_map} transitions away from it without triggering
181 // the "deoptimize dependent code" mechanism.
182 receiver_map->NotifyLeafMapLayoutChange(isolate);
183 // Finally, perform the map rollback.
184 receiver->synchronized_set_map(*parent_map);
185#if VERIFY_HEAP
186 receiver->HeapObjectVerify(isolate);
187 receiver->property_array().PropertyArrayVerify(isolate);
188#endif
189 return true;
190}
191
192} // namespace
193
194Maybe<bool> Runtime::DeleteObjectProperty(Isolate* isolate,
195 Handle<JSReceiver> receiver,
196 Handle<Object> key,
197 LanguageMode language_mode) {
198 if (DeleteObjectPropertyFast(isolate, receiver, key)) return Just(true);
199
200 bool success = false;
201 LookupIterator::Key lookup_key(isolate, key, &success);
202 if (!success) return Nothing<bool>();
203 LookupIterator it(isolate, receiver, lookup_key, LookupIterator::OWN);
204
205 return JSReceiver::DeleteProperty(&it, language_mode);
206}

.Initialize(trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled281, "V8.Runtime_"

(args_length, args_object); return (__RT_impl_Runtime_ObjectHasOwnProperty

(int args_length, Address* args_object, Isolate* isolate) { (
(void) 0); ; if ((__builtin_expect(!!(TracingFlags::is_runtime_stats_enabled
()), 0))) { return Stats_Runtime_ObjectHasOwnProperty(args_length
, args_object, isolate); } RuntimeArguments args(args_length,
args_object); return (__RT_impl_Runtime_ObjectHasOwnProperty
(args, isolate)).ptr(); } static Object __RT_impl_Runtime_ObjectHasOwnProperty
(RuntimeArguments args, Isolate* isolate) {
282 HandleScope scope(isolate);
283 Handle<Object> property = args.at(1);
284
285 // TODO(ishell): To improve performance, consider performing the to-string
286 // conversion of {property} before calling into the runtime.
287 bool success;
288 LookupIterator::Key key(isolate, property, &success);
289 if (!success) return ReadOnlyRoots(isolate).exception();
290
291 Handle<Object> object = args.at(0);
292
293 if (object->IsJSModuleNamespace()) {
294 if (key.is_element()) {
295 // Namespace objects can't have indexed properties.
296 return ReadOnlyRoots(isolate).false_value();
297 }
298 LookupIterator it(isolate, object, key, LookupIterator::OWN);
299 PropertyDescriptor desc;
300 Maybe<bool> result = JSReceiver::GetOwnPropertyDescriptor(&it, &desc);
301 if (!result.IsJust()) return ReadOnlyRoots(isolate).exception();
302 return isolate->heap()->ToBoolean(result.FromJust());
303
304 } else if (object->IsJSObject()) {
305 Handle<JSObject> js_obj = Handle<JSObject>::cast(object);
306 // Fast case: either the key is a real named property or it is not
307 // an array index and there are no interceptors or hidden
308 // prototypes.
309 // TODO(jkummerow): Make JSReceiver::HasOwnProperty fast enough to
310 // handle all cases directly (without this custom fast path).
311 {
312 LookupIterator::Configuration c = LookupIterator::OWN_SKIP_INTERCEPTOR;
313 LookupIterator it(isolate, js_obj, key, js_obj, c);
314 Maybe<bool> maybe = JSReceiver::HasProperty(&it);
315 if (maybe.IsNothing()) return ReadOnlyRoots(isolate).exception();
316 DCHECK(!isolate->has_pending_exception())((void) 0);
317 if (maybe.FromJust()) return ReadOnlyRoots(isolate).true_value();
318 }
319
320 Map map = js_obj->map();
321 if (!map.IsJSGlobalProxyMap() &&
322 (key.is_element() && key.index() <= JSArray::kMaxArrayIndex
323 ? !map.has_indexed_interceptor()
324 : !map.has_named_interceptor())) {
325 return ReadOnlyRoots(isolate).false_value();
326 }
327
328 // Slow case.
329 LookupIterator it(isolate, js_obj, key, js_obj, LookupIterator::OWN);
330 Maybe<bool> maybe = JSReceiver::HasProperty(&it);
331 if (maybe.IsNothing()) return ReadOnlyRoots(isolate).exception();
332 DCHECK(!isolate->has_pending_exception())((void) 0);
333 return isolate->heap()->ToBoolean(maybe.FromJust());
334
335 } else if (object->IsJSProxy()) {
336 LookupIterator it(isolate, object, key, Handle<JSProxy>::cast(object),
337 LookupIterator::OWN);
338 Maybe<PropertyAttributes> attributes =
339 JSReceiver::GetPropertyAttributes(&it);
340 if (attributes.IsNothing()) return ReadOnlyRoots(isolate).exception();
341 return isolate->heap()->ToBoolean(attributes.FromJust() != ABSENT);
342
343 } else if (object->IsString()) {
344 return isolate->heap()->ToBoolean(
345 key.is_element()
346 ? key.index() < static_cast<size_t>(String::cast(*object).length())
347 : key.name()->Equals(ReadOnlyRoots(isolate).length_string()));
348 } else if (object->IsNullOrUndefined(isolate)) {
349 THROW_NEW_ERROR_RETURN_FAILURE(do { auto* __isolate__ = (isolate); return __isolate__->Throw
(*__isolate__->factory()->NewTypeError(MessageTemplate::
kUndefinedOrNullToObject)); } while (false)
350 isolate, NewTypeError(MessageTemplate::kUndefinedOrNullToObject))do { auto* __isolate__ = (isolate); return __isolate__->Throw
(*__isolate__->factory()->NewTypeError(MessageTemplate::
kUndefinedOrNullToObject)); } while (false);
351 }
352
353 return ReadOnlyRoots(isolate).false_value();
354}

(RuntimeArguments args, Isolate* isolate); __attribute__((noinline
)) static Address Stats_Runtime_GetProperty(int args_length, Address
* args_object, Isolate* isolate) { RuntimeCallTimerScope timer
(isolate, RuntimeCallCounterId::kRuntime_GetProperty); static

(trace_event_unique_category_group_enabled583, "V8.Runtime_" "Runtime_GetProperty"
, h); }; RuntimeArguments args(args_length, args_object); return
(__RT_impl_Runtime_GetProperty(args, isolate)).ptr(); } Address
Runtime_GetProperty(int args_length, Address* args_object, Isolate
* isolate) { ((void) 0); ; if ((__builtin_expect(!!(TracingFlags
::is_runtime_stats_enabled()), 0))) { return Stats_Runtime_GetProperty
(args_length, args_object, isolate); } RuntimeArguments args(
args_length, args_object); return (__RT_impl_Runtime_GetProperty
(args, isolate)).ptr(); } static Object __RT_impl_Runtime_GetProperty
(RuntimeArguments args, Isolate* isolate) {
584 HandleScope scope(isolate);
585 DCHECK_EQ(2, args.length())((void) 0);
586 CONVERT_ARG_HANDLE_CHECKED(Object, receiver_obj, 0)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(args[0].IsObject())), 0))) { V8_Fatal
("Check failed: %s.", "args[0].IsObject()"); } } while (false
); Handle<Object> receiver_obj = args.at<Object>(
0);;
587 CONVERT_ARG_HANDLE_CHECKED(Object, key_obj, 1)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(args[1].IsObject())), 0))) { V8_Fatal
("Check failed: %s.", "args[1].IsObject()"); } } while (false
); Handle<Object> key_obj = args.at<Object>(1);;
588
589 // Fast cases for getting named properties of the receiver JSObject
590 // itself.
591 //
592 // The global proxy objects has to be excluded since LookupOwn on
593 // the global proxy object can return a valid result even though the
594 // global proxy object never has properties. This is the case
595 // because the global proxy object forwards everything to its hidden
596 // prototype including own lookups.
597 //
598 // Additionally, we need to make sure that we do not cache results
599 // for objects that require access checks.
600
601 // Convert string-index keys to their number variant to avoid internalization
602 // below; and speed up subsequent conversion to index.
603 uint32_t index;
604 if (key_obj->IsString() && String::cast(*key_obj).AsArrayIndex(&index)) {
605 key_obj = isolate->factory()->NewNumberFromUint(index);
606 }
607 if (receiver_obj->IsJSObject()) {
608 if (!receiver_obj->IsJSGlobalProxy() &&
609 !receiver_obj->IsAccessCheckNeeded() && key_obj->IsName()) {
610 Handle<JSObject> receiver = Handle<JSObject>::cast(receiver_obj);
611 Handle<Name> key = Handle<Name>::cast(key_obj);
612 key_obj = key = isolate->factory()->InternalizeName(key);
613
614 DisallowHeapAllocation no_allocation;
615 if (receiver->IsJSGlobalObject()) {
616 // Attempt dictionary lookup.
617 GlobalDictionary dictionary =
618 JSGlobalObject::cast(*receiver).global_dictionary();
619 InternalIndex entry = dictionary.FindEntry(isolate, key);
620 if (entry.is_found()) {
621 PropertyCell cell = dictionary.CellAt(entry);
622 if (cell.property_details().kind() == kData) {
623 Object value = cell.value();
624 if (!value.IsTheHole(isolate)) return value;
625 // If value is the hole (meaning, absent) do the general lookup.
626 }
627 }
628 } else if (!receiver->HasFastProperties()) {
629 // Attempt dictionary lookup.
630 NameDictionary dictionary = receiver->property_dictionary();
631 InternalIndex entry = dictionary.FindEntry(isolate, key);
632 if ((entry.is_found()) &&
633 (dictionary.DetailsAt(entry).kind() == kData)) {
634 return dictionary.ValueAt(entry);
635 }
636 }
637 } else if (key_obj->IsSmi()) {
638 // JSObject without a name key. If the key is a Smi, check for a
639 // definite out-of-bounds access to elements, which is a strong indicator
640 // that subsequent accesses will also call the runtime. Proactively
641 // transition elements to FAST_*_ELEMENTS to avoid excessive boxing of
642 // doubles for those future calls in the case that the elements would
643 // become PACKED_DOUBLE_ELEMENTS.
644 Handle<JSObject> js_object = Handle<JSObject>::cast(receiver_obj);
645 ElementsKind elements_kind = js_object->GetElementsKind();
646 if (IsDoubleElementsKind(elements_kind)) {
647 if (Smi::ToInt(*key_obj) >= js_object->elements().length()) {
648 elements_kind = IsHoleyElementsKind(elements_kind) ? HOLEY_ELEMENTS
649 : PACKED_ELEMENTS;
650 JSObject::TransitionElementsKind(js_object, elements_kind);
651 }
652 } else {
653 DCHECK(IsSmiOrObjectElementsKind(elements_kind) ||((void) 0)
654 !IsFastElementsKind(elements_kind))((void) 0);
655 }
656 }
657 } else if (receiver_obj->IsString() && key_obj->IsSmi()) {
658 // Fast case for string indexing using [] with a smi index.
659 Handle<String> str = Handle<String>::cast(receiver_obj);
660 int index = Handle<Smi>::cast(key_obj)->value();
661 if (index >= 0 && index < str->length()) {
662 Factory* factory = isolate->factory();
663 return *factory->LookupSingleCharacterStringFromCode(
664 String::Flatten(isolate, str)->Get(index));
665 }
666 }
667
668 // Fall back to GetObjectProperty.
669 RETURN_RESULT_OR_FAILURE(do { Handle<Object> __result__; Isolate* __isolate__ = (
isolate); if (!(Runtime::GetObjectProperty(isolate, receiver_obj
, key_obj)).ToHandle(&__result__)) { ((void) 0); return ReadOnlyRoots
(__isolate__).exception(); } ((void) 0); return *__result__; }
while (false)
670 isolate, Runtime::GetObjectProperty(isolate, receiver_obj, key_obj))do { Handle<Object> __result__; Isolate* __isolate__ = (
isolate); if (!(Runtime::GetObjectProperty(isolate, receiver_obj
, key_obj)).ToHandle(&__result__)) { ((void) 0); return ReadOnlyRoots
(__isolate__).exception(); } ((void) 0); return *__result__; }
while (false);
671}

) 0); ; if ((__builtin_expect(!!(TracingFlags::is_runtime_stats_enabled

(RuntimeArguments args, Isolate* isolate) {
850 HandleScope scope(isolate);
851 DCHECK_EQ(1, args.length())((void) 0);
852 CONVERT_ARG_HANDLE_CHECKED(Object, object, 0)do { if ((__builtin_expect(!!(!(args[0].IsObject())), 0))) { V8_Fatal
("Check failed: %s.", "args[0].IsObject()"); } } while (false
); Handle<Object> object = args.at<Object>(0);;
853 if (!object->IsJSObject()) return Smi::zero();
854 Handle<JSObject> js_object = Handle<JSObject>::cast(object);
855 // It could have been a DCHECK but we call this function directly from tests.
856 if (!js_object->map().is_deprecated()) return Smi::zero();
857 // This call must not cause lazy deopts, because it's called from deferred
858 // code where we can't handle lazy deopts for lack of a suitable bailout
859 // ID. So we just try migration and signal failure if necessary,
860 // which will also trigger a deopt.
861 if (!JSObject::TryMigrateInstance(isolate, js_object)) return Smi::zero();
862 return *object;
863}

906 if (nexus.ic_state() == UNINITIALIZED) {

920 DataPropertyInLiteralFlags flags(flag);
921 PropertyAttributes attrs = (flags & DataPropertyInLiteralFlag::kDontEnum)
922 ? PropertyAttributes::DONT_ENUM
923 : PropertyAttributes::NONE;
924
925 if (flags & DataPropertyInLiteralFlag::kSetFunctionName) {
926 DCHECK(value->IsJSFunction())((void) 0);

929 Handle<Map> function_map(function->map(), isolate);
930 if (!JSFunction::SetName(function, name,
931 isolate->factory()->empty_string())) {
932 return ReadOnlyRoots(isolate).exception();
933 }
934 // Class constructors do not reserve in-object space for name field.
